index=\"-1\"><div class=\"overlay\"></div><div class=\"slide__content container\"><h3 class=\"heading--main center-content white-text\">Easy Breakfast Recipes to Refuel After a Good Night's Sleep</h3><p class=\"p--large center-content white-text only-visible-above-xs--block\">You've heard the saying: “Breakfast is the most important meal of the day.” Whoever came up with this well-known phrase wasn’t kidding. After getting a good night’s rest, you’ll need to fuel your body to ensure productivity throughout the day—so your usual cup of coffee alone just won’t cut it.</p><div class=\"center-content\"><a class=\"btn banner__btn center-content\" href=\"https://sleep.org/articles/easy-breakfast-recipes/\">Learn More</a></div></div></div><div class=\"slide js-welcome-hero background--hero-evening slick-slide slick-active\" index=\"0\" style=\"width: 785px;\"><div class=\"container header-offset\"><div class=\"heading__line--white heading__line--push-down\"></div><h1 class=\"heading--main--jumbo center-content white-text all-caps\">Good <span class=\"js-welcome-time\">Evening</span></h1><p class=\"p--large center-content white-text\"> Here at Sleep.org by the National Sleep Foundation we are dedicated to starting a movement about the positive benefits of sleep health. Learn more about how you can feel better and start improving your sleep today.</p><h4 class=\"white-text center-content heading--ital only-visible-above-xs--block\">&nbsp;</h4> <a class=\"icon-down-open scroll-down-arrow center-content only-visible-above-sm--block\" href=\"#sleep-health\"></a></div></div><div class=\"slide header-offset slick-slide\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;https://sleep.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Sleeping-at-Work-Companies-with-Nap-Rooms-and-Snooze-Friendly-Policies.jpg&quot;); width: 785px;\" index=\"1\"><div class=\"overlay\"></div><div class=\"slide__content container\"><h3 class=\"heading--main center-content white-text\">Sleeping at Work: Companies with Nap Rooms and Snooze-Friendly Policies</h3><p class=\"p--large center-content white-text only-visible-above-xs--block\">Sleeping on the job was once considered taboo, but today, more and more companies are encouraging employees to take a mid-shift snooze.</p><div class=\"center-content\"><a class=\"btn banner__btn center-content\" href=\"https://sleep.org/articles/sleeping-work-companies-nap-rooms-snooze-friendly-policies/\">Learn More</a></div></div></div><div class=\"slide header-offset slick-slide\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;https://sleep.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/The-Best-Sleep-Position-for-Your-Body.jpg&quot;); width: 785px;\" index=\"2\"><div class=\"overlay\"></div><div class=\"slide__content container\"><h3 class=\"heading--main center-content white-text\">The Best Sleep Position for Your Body</h3><p class=\"p--large center-content white-text only-visible-above-xs--block\">Your sleeping pose can have a major impact on your slumber—as well as your overall health. Poor p.m. posture could potentially cause back and neck pain, fatigue, sleep apnea, muscle cramping, and more.</p><div class=\"center-content\"><a class=\"btn banner__btn center-content\" href=\"https://sleep.org/articles/best-sleep-position/\">Learn More</a></div></div></div><div class=\"slide header-offset slick-slide\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;https://sleep.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Wearing-Socks-to-Bed-Is-it-Normal_.jpg&quot;); width: 785px;\" index=\"3\"><div class=\"overlay\"></div><div class=\"slide__content container\"><h3 class=\"heading--main center-content white-text\">Wearing Socks to Bed: Is it Normal?</h3><p class=\"p--large center-content white-text only-visible-above-xs--block\">Normal or not, wearing socks may be smart if you’re having trouble falling asleep. col-sm-offset-1 body-parts__info-container\"><div class=\"body-parts__info active\"><div class=\"body-parts__info__inner\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital--large heading--green\">Explore</h4><p class=\"p--large\">Click a body part to learn more about how sleep effects it.</p></div></div><div class=\"body-parts__info\" data-part=\"brain\"><div class=\"body-parts__info__inner\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital--large heading--green\">Brain</h4><p class=\"p--large\">Cerebral spinal fluid is pumped more quickly throughout the brain while you sleep. It acts like a dishwasher, whisking away waste products that brain cells make. So you wake up with, quite literally, a clean slate.</p></div></div><div class=\"body-parts__info\" data-part=\"heart\"><div class=\"body-parts__info__inner\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital--large heading--green\">Heart</h4><p class=\"p--large\">One body part that gets a break during sleep is your heart. Your ticker works hard during the day, so at night during non-REM sleep it takes some pressure off itself by reducing heart rate, as well as blood pressure.</p></div></div><div class=\"body-parts__info\" data-part=\"lungs\"><div class=\"body-parts__info__inner\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital--large heading--green\">Lungs</h4><p class=\"p--large\">When you’re awake, your breathing patterns vary greatly. You’ll breathe faster when excited and harder while exercising, for example. But during sleep, your breathing slows down and becomes very regular.</p></div></div><div class=\"body-parts__info\" data-part=\"stomach\"><div class=\"body-parts__info__inner\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital--large heading--green\">Stomach</h4><p class=\"p--large\">Certain foods contain an amino acid called tryptophan that causes sleepiness. Carbohydrates make tryptophan more available to the brain, which is why carbohydrate-heavy meals can make you drowsy.</p></div></div><div class=\"body-parts__info\" data-part=\"muscles\"><div class=\"body-parts__info__inner\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital--large heading--green\">Muscles</h4><p class=\"p--large\">While you sleep, your body releases growth hormones that work to rebuild muscles and joints. The more sleep you get, the better equipped your body will be to repair itself.</p></div></div></div></div><div class=\"center-content btn__container col-sm-12\"> <a class=\"btn btn--black\" href=\"https://sleep.org/topic/sleep-science/\">Learn More</a></div></section><section class=\"js-homepage-section\" data-topic=\"bedroom\" id=\"topic-bedroom\"><div class=\"descending-turq\"><div class=\"container center-content white-text\"><div class=\"col-sm-10 col-md-6 center-block\"><h1 class=\"heading--main all-caps\"><div class=\"icon-bedroom-bed section-icon\"></div>Bedroom<div class=\"heading__line--push-up heading__line--white\"></div></h1><p class=\"heading--tertiary\"></p><p class=\"p1\">Where you sleep matters. Design a bedroom that will help you drift off into dreamland.</p><p></p></div></div></div><div class=\"container-full descending-turq\"><div class=\"container white-text\"><div class=\"col-md-10 col-md-offset-1\"><div class=\"col-sm-3 col-md-2\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital--large center-content\">Touch</h4><div class=\"circle-icon--dashed center-block icon--spin\"><div class=\"icon-bedroom-touch icon--counterspin\"></div></div></div><div class=\"data-callout__line col-sm-1 col-md-offset-2 center-content\"></div><div class=\"row col-sm-7 col-md-5 col-sm-offset-1 col-md-offset-2 no-gutter-left no-gutter-right\"> <span class=\"col-xs-5 col-sm-8 data-callout\">91</span> <span class=\"col-xs-7 col-sm-12 p--large\">of Americans change their sheets every two weeks.</span></div></div></div></div><div class=\"container-full descending-turq\"><div class=\"container white-text\"><div class=\"col-md-10 col-md-offset-1\"><div class=\"col-sm-3 col-md-2\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital--large center-content\">See</h4><div class=\"circle-icon--dashed center-block icon--spin\"><div class=\"icon-glasses icon--counterspin\"></div></div></div><div class=\"data-callout__line col-sm-1 col-md-offset-2 center-content\"></div><div class=\"row col-sm-7 col-md-5 col-sm-offset-1 col-md-offset-2 no-gutter-left no-gutter-right\"> <span class=\"col-xs-5 col-sm-12 data-callout\">35</span> <span class=\"col-xs-7 col-sm-12 p--large\">of Americans don’t use bedroom curtains or shades.</span></div></div></div></div><div class=\"container-full descending-turq\"><div class=\"container white-text\"><div class=\"col-md-10 col-md-offset-1\"><div class=\"col-sm-3 col-md-2\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital--large center-content\">Hear</h4><div class=\"circle-icon--dashed center-block icon--spin\"><div class=\"icon-bedroom-hear icon--counterspin\"></div></div></div><div class=\"data-callout__line col-sm-1 col-md-offset-2 center-content\"></div><div class=\"row col-sm-7 col-md-5 col-sm-offset-1 col-md-offset-2 no-gutter-left no-gutter-right\"> <span class=\"col-xs-5 col-sm-12 data-callout\">5</span> <span class=\"col-xs-7 col-sm-12 p--large\">of Americans use a sound conditioner in their bedrooms.</span></div></div></div></div><div class=\"container-full descending-turq\"><div class=\"container white-text\"><div class=\"col-md-10 col-md-offset-1\"><div class=\"col-sm-3 col-md-2\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital--large center-content\">Smell</h4><div class=\"circle-icon--dashed center-block icon--spin\"><div class=\"icon-bedroom-smell icon--counterspin\"></div></div></div><div class=\"data-callout__line col-sm-1 col-md-offset-2 center-content\"></div><div class=\"row col-sm-7 col-md-5 col-sm-offset-1 col-md-offset-2 no-gutter-left no-gutter-right\"> <span class=\"col-xs-5 col-sm-12 data-callout\">91</span> <span class=\"col-xs-7 col-sm-12 p--large\">of Americans prefer sheets with a fresh scent.</span></div></div></div></div><div class=\"container-full descending-turq\"><div class=\"container white-text\"><div class=\"col-md-10 col-md-offset-1\"><div class=\"col-sm-3 col-md-2\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital--large center-content\">Taste</h4><div class=\"circle-icon--dashed center-block icon--spin\"><div class=\"icon-bedroom-taste icon--counterspin\"></div></div></div><div class=\"data-callout__line col-sm-1 col-md-offset-2 center-content\"></div><div class=\"row col-sm-7 col-md-5 col-sm-offset-1 col-md-offset-2 no-gutter-left no-gutter-right\"> <span class=\"col-xs-5 col-sm-12 data-callout\">78</span> <span class=\"col-xs-7 col-sm-12 p--large\">of Americans have at least one caffeinated beverage a day.</span></div></div><div class=\"center-content btn__container col-sm-12\"> <a class=\"btn btn--white\" href=\"https://sleep.org/topic/bedroom/\">Learn More</a></div></div></div></section><section class=\"container js-homepage-section\" data-topic=\"lifestyle\" id=\"topic-lifestyle\"><h1 class=\"heading--main center-content all-caps\"><div class=\"icon-cup section-icon\"></div>Lifestyle<div class=\"heading__line--push-up\"></div></h1><div class=\"col-sm-10 col-md-6 center-block\"><p class=\"heading--tertiary center-content\"></p><p class=\"p1\">From work to weekend schedules, our everyday lives impact our sleep…and vice versa.</p><p></p></div><div class=\"row col-md-11 center-block lifestyle-interactive-block\"><div class=\"col-sm-6 col-md-6 col-lg-4\"><div class=\"revealer\"><div class=\"revealer__face\"><div class=\"revealer__face__row\"><div class=\"revealer__face__cell\"><div class=\"circle-icon--gray icon-bedroom-taste center-block\"></div></div></div><div class=\"revealer__face__row\"><div class=\"revealer__face__cell\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital\">Snooze Foods &amp; Pick-Me-Ups</h4></div></div></div><div class=\"revealer__drawer\"><h4 class=\"heading--small-bold white-text\">Tryptophan</h4><p class=\"white-text\">Tryptophan causes sleepiness. Proteins from the food we eat are the building blocks of tryptophan, which is why the best bedtime snack is one that contains both a carbohydrate and protein such as cereal with milk.</p></div></div></div><div class=\"col-sm-6 col-md-6 col-lg-4\"><div class=\"revealer\"><div class=\"revealer__face\"><div class=\"revealer__face__row\"><div class=\"revealer__face__cell\"><div class=\"circle-icon--gray icon-lifestyle-leaf center-block\"></div></div></div><div class=\"revealer__face__row\"><div class=\"revealer__face__cell\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital\">Nature's Sleeping Pill</h4></div></div></div><div class=\"revealer__drawer\"><h4 class=\"heading--small-bold white-text\">Melatonin</h4><p class=\"white-text\">Melatonin helps control your sleep-wake cycles. Your body’s internal clock (also known as your circadian rhythm) influences how much melatonin your body makes, as does the amount of light that you're exposed to each day.</p></div></div></div><div class=\"col-sm-6 col-md-6 col-lg-4\"><div class=\"revealer\"><div class=\"revealer__face\"><div class=\"revealer__face__row\"><div class=\"revealer__face__cell\"><div class=\"circle-icon--gray icon-heart center-block\"></div></div></div><div class=\"revealer__face__row\"><div class=\"revealer__face__cell\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital\">Sex: Sleep Aid or Thief?</h4></div></div></div><div class=\"revealer__drawer\"><h4 class=\"heading--small-bold white-text\">Sex</h4><p class=\"white-text\">Sex = good for sleep. It boosts oxytocin (a hormone that makes you feel connected to your partner) and lowers cortisol (a stress-related hormone). Plus, orgasms release prolactin, which help you feel relaxed and sleepy.</p></div></div></div><div class=\"col-sm-6 col-md-6 col-lg-4\"><div class=\"revealer\"><div class=\"revealer__face\"><div class=\"revealer__face__row\"><div class=\"revealer__face__cell\"><div class=\"circle-icon--gray icon-lifestyle-coffee-sleeve center-block\"></div></div></div><div class=\"revealer__face__row\"><div class=\"revealer__face__cell\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital\">That Afternoon Coffee Jolt</h4></div></div></div><div class=\"revealer__drawer\"><h4 class=\"heading--small-bold white-text\">Caffeine</h4><p class=\"white-text\">Generally, caffiene lasts for 5 to 6 hours in the body before wearing off. So cut out the coffee after early afternoon so that you can start to wind down in time for bedtime.</p></div></div></div><div class=\"col-sm-6 col-md-6 col-lg-4\"><div class=\"revealer\"><div class=\"revealer__face\"><div class=\"revealer__face__row\"><div class=\"revealer__face__cell\"><div class=\"circle-icon--gray icon-lifestyle-reaction-time center-block\"></div></div></div><div class=\"revealer__face__row\"><div class=\"revealer__face__cell\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital\">Stay Sharp</h4></div></div></div><div class=\"revealer__drawer\"><h4 class=\"heading--small-bold white-text\">Reaction Time</h4><p class=\"white-text\">Sleep improves your ability to make more accurate split-second decisions by about four percent. Hey, it may not sound like much, but every little bit helps!</p></div></div></div><div class=\"col-sm-6 col-md-6 col-lg-4\"><div class=\"revealer\"><div class=\"revealer__face\"><div class=\"revealer__face__row\"><div class=\"revealer__face__cell\"><div class=\"circle-icon--gray icon-run center-block\"></div></div></div><div class=\"revealer__face__row\"><div class=\"revealer__face__cell\"><h4 class=\"heading--ital\">Work Out, Sleep Better</h4></div></div></div><div class=\"revealer__drawer\"><h4 class=\"heading--small-bold white-text\">Exercise</h4><p class=\"white-text\">It doesn't matter when you hit the gym, just that you get in your daily burn. People who work out regularly sleep better—and longer—than those who don't.</p></div></div></div></div><div class=\"center-content btn__container col-sm-12\"> <a class=\"btn btn--black\" href=\"https://sleep.org/topic/lifestyle/\">Learn More</a></div></section><section style=\"overflow: hidden\" class=\"container-full js-homepage-section background--yellow\" data-topic=\"age\" id=\"topic-age\"><div class=\"container\"><h1 class=\"heading--main center-content all-caps\"><div class=\"icon-age-people section-icon\"></div> Age<div class=\"heading__line--push-up\"></div></h1><div class=\"col-sm-10 col-md-6 center-block\"><p class=\"heading--tertiary center-content\"></p><p class=\"p1\">Sleep needs change as we age. class=\"rotary__center\"><div class=\"rotary__center__item active\"><h1 class=\"rotary__center__item__cell heading--main center-content\">How Much Sleep Do We Really Need?</h1></div><div class=\"rotary__center__item\" data-age=\"newborn\"><div class=\"rotary__center__item__cell\"><h2 class=\"heading--small-bold\">Newborns</h2><p>Newborns less than three months old sleep between 14 and 17 hours each day.</p><p class=\"appropriate\">As few as 11 hours and as many as 19 hours may be appropriate.</p></div></div><div class=\"rotary__center__item\" data-age=\"infant\"><div class=\"rotary__center__item__cell\"><h2 class=\"heading--small-bold\">Infants</h2><p>Infants (between 4 and 11 months old) sleep between 12 and 15 hours each day.</p><p class=\"appropriate\">As few as 10 hours and as many as 18 hours may be appropriate.</p></div></div><div class=\"rotary__center__item\" data-age=\"toddler\"><div class=\"rotary__center__item__cell\"><h2 class=\"heading--small-bold\">Toddlers</h2><p>Toddlers (between 1 and 2 years old) sleep between 11 and 14 hours each day.</p><p class=\"appropriate\">As few as 9 hours and as many as 16 hours may be appropriate.</p></div></div><div class=\"rotary__center__item\" data-age=\"preschool\"><div class=\"rotary__center__item__cell\"><h2 class=\"heading--small-bold\">Preschoolers</h2><p>Preschoolers (between 3 and 5 years old) sleep between 10 and 13 hours each day.</p><p class=\"appropriate\">As few as 8 hours and as many as 14 hours may be appropriate.</p></div></div><div class=\"rotary__center__item\" data-age=\"school\"><div class=\"rotary__center__item__cell\"><h2 class=\"heading--small-bold\">School Age Children</h2><p>School-aged children (6 to 13 years old) need 9 to 11 hours of sleep each day.</p><p class=\"appropriate\">As few as 7 hours and as many as 12 hours may be appropriate.</p></div></div><div class=\"rotary__center__item\" data-age=\"teen\"><div class=\"rotary__center__item__cell\"><h2 class=\"heading--small-bold\">Teens</h2><p>Teens (14 to 17 years old) need 8 to 10 hours each day to feel their best.</p><p class=\"appropriate\">As few as 7 hours and as many as 11 hours may be appropriate.</p></div></div><div class=\"rotary__center__item\" data-age=\"young_adult\"><div class=\"rotary__center__item__cell\"><h2 class=\"heading--small-bold\">Young Adults</h2><p>Young Adults (18 to 25 years old) need 7 to 9 hours each day to feel their best.</p><p class=\"appropriate\">As few as 6 hours and as many as 11 hours may be appropriate.</p></div></div><div class=\"rotary__center__item\" data-age=\"adult\"><div class=\"rotary__center__item__cell\"><h2 class=\"heading--small-bold\">Adults</h2><p>Adults need between 7 and 9 hours of sleep each day to feel their best.</p><p class=\"appropriate\">As few as 6 hours and as many as 10 hours may be appropriate.</p></div></div><div class=\"rotary__center__item\" data-age=\"older_adult\"><div class=\"rotary__center__item__cell\"><h2 class=\"heading--small-bold\">Older Adults</h2><p>Older Adults (65 years and older) need 7 to 8 hours each day to feel their best.</p><p class=\"appropriate\">As few as 5 hours and as many as 9 hours may be appropriate.</p></div></div></div></div><div class=\"age-slider row\"><div class=\"age-slider__slider class=\"rotary__center__item__cell\"><h2 class=\"heading--small-bold\">Teens</h2><p>Teens (14 to 17 years old) need 8 to 10 hours each day to feel their best.</p><p class=\"appropriate\">As few as 7 hours and as many as 11 hours may be appropriate.</p></div></div><div class=\"rotary__center__item\" data-age=\"young_adult\"><div class=\"rotary__center__item__cell\"><h2 class=\"heading--small-bold\">Young Adults</h2><p>Young Adults (18 to 25 years old) need 7 to 9 hours each day to feel their best.</p><p class=\"appropriate\">As few as 6 hours and as many as 11 hours may be appropriate.</p></div></div><div class=\"rotary__center__item\" data-age=\"adult\"><div class=\"rotary__center__item__cell\"><h2 class=\"heading--small-bold\">Adults</h2><p>Adults need between 7 and 9 hours of sleep each day to feel their best.</p><p class=\"appropriate\">As few as 6 hours and as many as 10 hours may be appropriate.</p></div></div><div class=\"rotary__center__item\" data-age=\"older_adult\"><div class=\"rotary__center__item__cell\"><h2 class=\"heading--small-bold\">Older Adults</h2><p>Older Adults (65 years and older) need 7 to 8 hours each day to feel their best.</p><p class=\"appropriate\">As few as 5 hours and as many as 9 hours may be appropriate.</p></div></div></div></div><div class=\"center-content btn__container btn__container--pull-up col-sm-12\"> <a class=\"btn btn--black\" href=\"https://sleep.org/topic/age/\">Learn More</a></div></div></section><section class=\"homepage-quiz container js-homepage-section\" data-topic=\"profile\"
